  "${CMAKE_CURRENT_LIST_DIR}/Inkplate-6-Arduino-library/examples/Inkplate10/Advanced_Inkplate_Features/Inkplate_Battery_Voltage_And_Temperature/symbols.h"
  "${CMAKE_CURRENT_LIST_DIR}/Inkplate-6-Arduino-library/examples/Inkplate10/Advanced_Inkplate_Features/Inkplate_Low_Power/picture2.h"
  "${CMAKE_CURRENT_LIST_DIR}/Inkplate-6-Arduino-library/examples/Inkplate10/Advanced_Inkplate_Features/Inkplate_Low_Power/picture3.h"
  "${CMAKE_CURRENT_LIST_DIR}/Inkplate-6-Arduino-library/examples/Inkplate10/Advanced_Inkplate_Features/Inkplate_Low_Power/picture1.h"
  "${CMAKE_CURRENT_LIST_DIR}/Inkplate-6-Arduino-library/examples/Inkplate10/Advanced_Inkplate_Features/Inkplate_Bluetooth_Peripheral_Mode_Example/Peripheral.h"
  "${CMAKE_CURRENT_LIST_DIR}/Inkplate-6-Arduino-library/examples/Inkplate10/Others/Inkplate_Factory_Programming_VCOM/image.h"
)

target_include_directories(pac-inkplatelibrary INTERFACE
 "${CMAKE_CURRENT_LIST_DIR}/Inkplate-6-Arduino-library/src"
)

if (NOT TARGET arduino-compat)
    add_subdirectory(../../arduino-compat build_arduino-compat)
endif()

if (NOT TARGET pac-adafruit-gfx-library)
    add_subdirectory(../../libs/adafruit-gfx-library build_pac-adafruit-gfx-library)
endif()

target_link_libraries(pac-inkplatelibrary INTERFACE
    arduino-compat
    pac-adafruit-gfx-library
)
